comprehensive pluggable health check system. The main framework is in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/healthz/healthz.go` with three separate handler installation functions: `InstallHandler` (for /healthz), `InstallReadyzHandler` (for /readyz), and `InstallLivezHandler` (for /livez).\\n\\n**Core Health Checks:**\\n1. **PingHealthz** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/healthz/healthz.go) - Simple ping that always succeeds\\n2. **LogHealthz** - Checks if logging is not blocked by verifying klog can flush within 2 minutes\\n3. **NewInformerSyncHealthz** - Verifies that all Kubernetes informers (cache watchers) have completed initial synchronization\\n4. **NewShutdownHealthz** - Checks if a shutdown signal has been received\\n5. **ETcd Health Checks** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/etcd.go) - Direct connectivity checks to etcd storage backend, supporting both primary and override server configurations\\n\\nIn `cmd/kube-scheduler/app/server.go` (line 372-376), the scheduler registers health checks using `InstallHandler`, `InstallLivezHandler`, and `InstallReadyzHandler`. The framework in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/config.go` (line 398) establishes default checks of PingHealthz and LogHealthz.\\n\\nThe `/readyz` endpoint specifically includes ETcd readiness checks via `AddReadyzChecks` in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/etcd.go` (lines 367-369), which validates that the API server can communicate with its etcd backend.\\n\\n### Prometheus (github.com/prometheus/prometheus)\\n**Endpoints:** `/-/healthy`, `/-/ready`\\n\\nPrometheus uses a simpler state-based approach in `web/web.go`. The `testReady()` function (web/web.go line 659) wraps handler functions to enforce readiness state before allowing requests, making it a gating mechanism for query serving rather than a composite health check.\\n\\n### Grafana (github.com/grafana/grafana)\\n**Endpoints:** `/healthz`, `/readyz`, `/livez`\\n\\nGrafana implements health checks through its embedded Kubernetes API server. In `pkg/services/apiserver/service.go` (lines 211-214), the health endpoints are registered as route groups that proxy to the underlying `genericapiserver.GenericAPIServer`.\\n\\nThe implementation registers these routes in `ProvideService()` with a proxy handler that:\\n1. Waits for the service to be running via `AwaitRunning()`\\n2. Delegates to the Kubernetes API server handler\\n3. Inherits the full Kubernetes health check framework\\n\\nThis means Grafana's `/healthz`, `/readyz`, and `/livez` endpoints support the same pluggable health checks as Kubernetes, though the specific checks depend on which API server components are registered.\\n\\n## Key Architectural Differences\\n\\n**Kubernetes:** Pluggable, component-specific health checks (ping, logging, informers, etcd connectivity, shutdown signal). Each check can be excluded or grouped, with detailed failure reporting.\\n\\n**Prometheus:** State-based readiness (Ready/NotReady/Stopping) without granular component checks.
